   kailāsaśikharāsīnaṃ bhairavaṃ vigatāmayam /	kElAsa SiKara AsInam BEravam vigata Amayam /

   yogādyaṃ layaparyantaṃ dhāmnā caivātra pūrvavat /	yoga Adyam laya paryantam DAmnA ca eva atra pUrvavat /
   śikhayā śatahomāttu vidyāyā niṣkṛtirbhavet // SvaT_4.178 //	SiKayA Sata homAt tu vidyAyAH nizkRtiH Bavet // SvaT_4.178 //
   praṇavādi tato rudram āvāhya sthāpya pūjayet /	praNava Adi tatas rudram AvAhya sTApya pUjayet /

   puryaṣakāṃśaṃ vinyasya visarjya rudradevatām /	puryazaka aMSam vinyasya visarjya rudra devatAm /

   hrasvadīrghavibhāgena vidyāṃ śāntau niyojayet /	hrasva dIrGa viBAgena vidyAm SAntO niyojayet /

   padaikādaśikā jñeyā purāṇi daśa sapta ca /	padA ekAdaSikA jQeyA purANi daSa sapta ca /

   ahaṃkāraṃ tathāpyevaṃ hutvedaṃ kṣamayettataḥ /	ahaMkAram taTA api evam hutvA idam kzamayet tatas /

   tadvoditvā vimucyeta gatvā bhūyo na jāyate /	tat vA uditvA vimucyeta gatvA BUyas na jAyate /
   adhvaṣṭkaṃ yathā prāṇe saṃsthitaṃ kathayāmi te // SvaT_4.241 //	aDvazwkam yaTA prANe saMsTitam kaTayAmi te // SvaT_4.241 //

   bhuvanādhvā sa vijñeyas tattvādhvā ca tathaiva hi // SvaT_4.242 //	Buvana aDvA sa vijQeyaH tattva aDvA ca taTA eva hi // SvaT_4.242 //
   kalākalitasaṃtānaḥ prāṇaḥ saṃcarate sadā /	kalA kalita saMtAnaH prANaH saMcarate sadA /

   evaṃ bindukalā jñeyā nādaśaktyātmikāśca yāḥ /	evam bindu kalAH jQeyAH nAda Sakti AtmikAH ca yAH /

   nādho nirīkṣate bhūyaḥ śivatattvaṃ gato yadā /	na aDas nirIkzate BUyas Siva tattvam gataH yadA /
   adho vai yātyadharmeṇa dharmeṇordhvaṃ vrajetpunaḥ // SvaT_4.250 //	aDas vE yAti aDarmeNa DarmeNa UrDvam vrajet punar // SvaT_4.250 //

   ekāśītipadānyeva vidyārājasthitānyapi /	ekASIti padAni eva vidyA rAja sTitAni api /

   tasmādevaṃ padānyatra tāni prāṇakrameṇa tu /	tasmAt evam padAni atra tAni prANa krameNa tu /

   mantrikādaśikā yā tu sā ca haṃse vyavasthitā /	mantrikAdaSikA yA tu sA ca haMse vyavasTitAH /

   akāraśca ukāraśca makāro bindureva ca /	akAraH ca ukAraH ca makAraH binduH eva ca /

   śabdo jyotiḥ tato mantrāḥ kāraṇā bhuvanāni ca /	SabdaH jyotiH tatas mantrAH kAraNAH BuvanAni ca /

   unmanyante pare yojyo na kālastatra vidyate /	unmanyante pare yojyaH na kAlaH tatra vidyate /
   nityo nityodito vyāpī ādirūpaṃ na saṃtyajet // SvaT_4.287 //	nityaH nityoditaH vyApI Adi rUpam na saMtyajet // SvaT_4.287 //

   setubandhaṃ ca taṃ mārgaṃ yatra gatvā na jāyate /	setu banDam ca tam mArgam yatra gatvA na jAyate /

   ete 'tra samatāṃ yānti anyathā tu pṛthak pṛthak /	ete atra sama tAm yAnti anyaTA tu pRTak pRTak /

   śaktimadhyagato nādaḥ śaktyātmā tu vidhīyate /	Sakti maDya gataH nAdaH Sakti AtmA tu viDIyate /

   tadūrdhvaṃ vyāpinīṃ prāpya sarvaṃ tanmayatāṃ vrajet /	tad UrDvam vyApinIm prApya sarvam tad maya tAm vrajet /
   samantādvyāpnuyādyasmād vyāpinītyabhidhīyate // SvaT_4.307 //	samantAt vyApnuyAt yasmAt vyApinI iti aBiDIyate // SvaT_4.307 //
   tadūrdhvaṃ samanāṃ vyāpya tanmayatvaṃ vrajetpunaḥ /	tad UrDvam samanAm vyApya tad maya tvam vrajet punar /
   sā ca sarvagatā jñeyā sāmarasyena saṃsthitā // SvaT_4.308 //	sA ca sarva gatA jQeyA sAmarasyena saMsTitAH // SvaT_4.308 //
   ṣaṣṭhaṃ samarasaṃ tyaktvā saptamaṃ tu tato vrajet /	zazWam sama rasam tyaktvA saptamam tu tatas vrajet /
   taṃ prāpya tanmayatvaṃ hi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā // SvaT_4.309 //	tam prApya tad maya tvam hi na atra kAryA vicAraNAH // SvaT_4.309 //
   sa ca sarveṣu bhūteṣu bhāvatatvendriyeṣu ca /	sa ca sarvezu BUtezu BAvatatva indriyezu ca /
   sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ caiva cetanācetanasthitam // SvaT_4.310 //	sTAvaram jaFgamam ca eva cetana acetana sTitam // SvaT_4.310 //
   adhvānaṃ vyāpya sarvaṃ tu sāmarasyena saṃsthitaḥ /	aDvAnam vyApya sarvam tu sAmarasyena saMsTitaH /
   prasahya cañcalītyeva yogināmapi yanmanaḥ // SvaT_4.311 //	prasahya caQcalI iti eva yoginAm api yat manaH // SvaT_4.311 //
   yasya jñeyamayo bhāvaḥ sthiraḥ pūrṇaḥ samantataḥ /	yasya jQeya mayaH BAvaH sTiraH pUrNaH samantataH /
   mano na calate tasya sarvāvasthāgatasya tu // SvaT_4.312 //	manaH na calate tasya sarva avasTA gatasya tu // SvaT_4.312 //
   yatra yatra mano yāti jñeyaṃ tatraiva cintayet /	yatra yatra manaH yAti jQeyam tatra eva cintayet /
   calitvā yāsyate kutra sarvaṃ śivamayaṃ yataḥ // SvaT_4.313 //	calitvA yAsyate kutra sarvam Siva mayam yatas // SvaT_4.313 //
   viṣayeṣu ca sarveṣu indriyārtheṣu ca sthitaḥ /	vizayezu ca sarvezu indriya arTezu ca sTitaH /
   yatra yatra nirūpyeta nāśivaṃ vidyate kvacit // SvaT_4.314 //	yatra yatra nirUpyeta na aSivam vidyate kvacid // SvaT_4.314 //
   evāṃ samarasaṃ jñātvā nāsau muhyet kadācana /	evAm sama rasam jQAtvA na asO muhyet kadAcana /
   yasyaivaṃ sarvato bhāvaḥ so 'pi sarvagato bhavet // SvaT_4.315 //	yasya evam sarvatas BAvaH saH api sarva gataH Bavet // SvaT_4.315 //
   evaṃ samarasaḥ prokto viṣuvattu nibodha me /	evam samarasaH proktaH vizuvat tu niboDa me /
   prathamaṃ prāṇaviṣuvan mātraṃ jñeyaṃ dvitīyakam // SvaT_4.316 //	praTamam prANa vizuvan mAtram jQeyam dvitIyakam // SvaT_4.316 //
   tṛtīyaṃ nāḍiviṣuvat praśāntaṃ ca caturthakam /	tRtIyam nAxi vizu vat praSAntam ca caturTakam /
   pañcamaṃ śaktiviṣuvat ṣaṣṭhaṃ vai kāla ucyate // SvaT_4.317 //	paQcamam Sakti vizuvat zazWam vE kAlaH ucyate // SvaT_4.317 //
   saptama tattvaviṣuvat pravibhāgastvathocyate /	saptama tattva vizuvat praviBAgaH tu aTa ucyate /

   prāṇe viṣuvadākhyātaṃ māntraṃ viṣuvaducyate /	prANe vizuvat AKyAtam mAntram vizuvat ucyate /

   parāparavibhāgena mantrātmā tu taducyate /	para apara viBAgena mantra AtmA tu tat ucyate /

   sarvāsāmeva nāḍīnāṃ madhye yā saṃvyavasthitā /	sarvAsAm eva nAxInAm maDye yA saMvyavasTitA /
   suṣumnā nāma sā jñeyā nābheḥ śaktyā śivaṃ gatā // SvaT_4.321 //	suzumnA nAma sA jQeyA nABeH SaktyA Sivam gatAH // SvaT_4.321 //
   tatra pravāhayennādaṃ nāḍīviṣuvaducyate /	tatra pravAhayet nAdam nAxI vizu vat ucyate /

   ayane ṣaḍaṅgulaścāraḥ kāraṇānyaṅgule 'ṅgule /	ayane zaz aFgulaH cAraH kAraNAni aFgule aFgule /
   tānyadhastātparityajya kāraṇāni ṣaḍeva tu // SvaT_4.323 //	tAni aDastAt parityajya kAraNAni zaz eva tu // SvaT_4.323 //
   saptame tu praśāntaṃ vai praśāntendriyagocaram /	saptame tu praSAntam vE praSAnta indriya gocaram /

   niścalo nistaraṅgaśca sthiraḥ pūrṇaḥ samantataḥ /	niScalaH nistaraFgaH ca sTiraH pUrNaH samantataH /

   etatpraśāntaviṣuvat śaktyupādhiṃ nibodha me /	etad praSAnta vizuvat Sakti upADim niboDa me /

   kālo bhrūkṣepamātrastu tatrānte kīrtito mayā /	kAlaH BrU kzepa mAtraH tu tatra ante kIrtitaH mayA /

   aparaḥ ṣoḍaśo yāvat kālaḥ saptadaśaḥ paraḥ /	aparaH zoxaSaH yAvat kAlaH saptadaSaH paraH /

   tṛtīyaḥ samanāsthāne tatkālaviṣuvatsmṛtam /	tRtIyaH samanA sTAne tad kAla vizu vat smRtam /
   etatṣaṣṭhaṃ samākhyātaṃ saptamaṃ tātvvamucyate // SvaT_4.331 //	etat zazWam samAKyAtam saptamam tAtu vam ucyate // SvaT_4.331 //
   unmanā parato devi tatrātmānaṃ niyojayet /	unmanA paratas devi tatra AtmAnam niyojayet /

   tattvākhyaṃ viṣuvaddevi sarveṣāṃ parataḥ sthitam /	tattva AKyam vizuvat devi sarvezAm paratas sTitam /
   viṣuvadevaṃvidhaṃ jñātvā ko na mucyeta bandhanāt // SvaT_4.333 //	vizuva devaMviDam jQAtvA kaH na mucyeta banDanAt // SvaT_4.333 //
   viṣuvatte samākhyātaṃ padārthabhedanaṃ śṛṇu /	vizuvat te samAKyAtam padArTa Bedanam SRNu /

   padārthaikādaśī jñeyā unmanāntaḥ paro bhavet /	padArTa ekAdaSI jQeyAH unmanAntaH paraH Bavet /

   evaṃ jñānena ca jñeyaṃ tasmin kuryāttu saṃsthitam /	evam jQAnena ca jQeyam tasmin kuryAt tu saMsTitam /
   jñānaṃ vai lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ jñeyatatvasya suvrate // SvaT_4.337 //	jQAnam vE lakzaNam proktam jQeyatatvasya suvrate // SvaT_4.337 //
   lakṣaṇaṃ guṇa ākhyātaḥ kalā tattvasya sarvadā /	lakzaNam guNaH AKyAtaH kalA tattvasya sarvadA /
   na guṇena vinā tattvaṃ na tattvena vinā guṇaḥ // SvaT_4.338 //	na guNena vinA tattvam na tattvena vinA guNaH // SvaT_4.338 //

   tvakcheṣe vyāpinī proktā samanā conmanā tataḥ /	tvac Seze vyApinI proktA sa manA ca unmanA tatas /

   bhedayenmatraśūlena mudrābhāvayutena ca /	Bedayet matra SUlena mudrA aBAva yutena ca /

   kaṇṭhastho viramecchabdaḥ kaṇṭhaṃ prāpya varānane /	kaNWa sTaH viramet SabdaH kaNWam prApya varAnane /
   bhindataḥ kaṇṭhadeśaṃ tu śabdo dhugadhugāyate // SvaT_4.371 //	BindataH kaNWa deSam tu SabdaH DugaDugAyate // SvaT_4.371 //
   tālumadhyagataḥ prāṇo yadā bhavati suvrate /	tAlu maDya gataH prANaH yadA Bavati suvrate /
   bindatastālugranthiṃ tu śabdo ghumaghumāyate // SvaT_4.372 //	bindataH tAlu granTim tu SabdaH GumaGumAyate // SvaT_4.372 //
   evaṃ te 'nubhavāḥ proktāḥ prāṇe carati suvrate /	evam te anuBavAH proktAH prANe carati suvrate /
   trayaste 'ṣṭakalāḥ proktā uparyuparitaḥ kramāt // SvaT_4.373 //	trayaH te azwa kalAH proktAH upari uparitas kramAt // SvaT_4.373 //
   tiṣṭhetsa yatra vai prāṇa ātmā tadgatimāpnuyāt /	tizWet sa yatra vE prANaH AtmA tad gatim ApnuyAt /

   ardhacandraṃ tu bhittvā vai bhedayettu nirodhinīm /	arDacandram tu BittvA vE Bedayet tu niroDinIm /

   sthanatrayamidaṃ devi pañcapañcakalānvitam /	sTana trayam idam devi paQca paQcakala anvitam /

   tattadrūpo bhavedātmā tāṃ tāṃ gatimavāpnuyāt /	tad tad rUpaH Bavet AtmA tAm tAm gatim avApnuyAt /
   nirodhinīṃ bhedayitvā tato nādaṃ vrajedbudhaḥ // SvaT_4.380 //	niroDinIm BedayitvA tatas nAdam vrajet buDaH // SvaT_4.380 //
   vaṃśaśabdasamaḥ śabdas tatra sūkṣmaḥ prajāyate /	vaMSa Sabda samaH SabdaH tatra sUkzmaH prajAyate /

   śaktiṃ bhitvā tato devi yaccheṣaṃ vyāpinī bhavet /	Saktim BitvA tatas devi yat Sezam vyApinI Bavet /

   sthānatrayamidaṃ devi pañcapañcakalānvitam /	sTAna trayam idam devi paQca paQcakala anvitam /

   bhitvā vai vyāpinīṃ devi samanāyāṃ manastyajet /	BitvA vE vyApinIm devi samanAyAm manaH tyajet /

   bandhanāśeṣanirmuktaḥ sattāmātrasvarūpakaḥ // SvaT_4.388 //	banDana aSeza nirmuktaH sattA mAtra svarUpakaH // SvaT_4.388 //

   gṛhāṇāti nāparaṃ bhāvaṃ na paraṃ ca śivātmakam // SvaT_4.389 //	gRhANa ati na aparam BAvam na param ca Siva Atmakam // SvaT_4.389 //

   ta ātmopāsakāḥ śaive na gacchanti paraṃ śivam /	te Atma upAsakAH SEve na gacCanti param Sivam /

   supradīpte yathā vahnau śikhā dṛśyeta cāmbare /	su pradIpte yaTA vahnO SiKA dRSyeta ca ambare /

   tadvadevābhimānastu kartavyo daiśikottamaiḥ /	tadvat eva aBimAnaH tu kartavyaH dESika uttamEH /

   matprāṇe sa tu paśvātmā līnaḥ samarasīgataḥ /	mad prANe sa tu paSu AtmA lInaH samarasI gataH /
   mantrakaraṇakriyāyogād yojayāmi pare śive // SvaT_4.400 //	mantra karaNa kriyA yogAt yojayAmi pare Sive // SvaT_4.400 //
   evaṃ yo vetti tattvena agnivaddehamadhyataḥ /	evam yaH vetti tattvena agni vat deha maDyatas /

   saṃkṣepeṇa tu tattvasya vyāptiṃ śṛṇu sureśvari // SvaT_4.404 //	saMkzepeNa tu tattvasya vyAptim SRNu sureSvari // SvaT_4.404 //
   vidyātattvāspadaṃ baddhvā bindutattvāsane sthitaḥ /	vidyA tattva Aspadam badDvA bindu tattva Asane sTitaH /

   sarvajñatvāvabodhena samanāntaścarā tu sā /	sarvajQa tva avaboDena samanAntaH carA tu sA /

   ato dharmisvabhāvo hi śivaḥ śāntaśca paṭhyate /	atas Darmi svaBAvaH hi SivaH SAntaH ca paWyate /

   pare caiva niyuktasya sruvamāpūrayetpunaḥ /	pare ca eva niyuktasya sruvam ApUrayet punar /
   sruco randhreṇa taddravyaṃ yāvadvahnau prayujyate // SvaT_4.438 //	srucaH ranDreNa tat dravyam yAvat vahnO prayujyate // SvaT_4.438 //
   bahisthāṃ kumbhakaṃ tāvat pare tattve tu bhāvayet /	bahi sTAm kumBakam tAvat pare tattve tu BAvayet /

   na nindedbhairavaṃ devaṃ śāstraṃ vānyasamudbhavam /	na nindet BEravam devam SAstram vA anya samudBavam /

   carukaṃ prāśayannityaṃ gurūn sampūjayet sadā /	carukam prASayat nityam gurUn sampUjayet sadA /

   adīkṣitānāṃ purato noccarecchāstrapaddhatim /	adIkzitAnAm puratas na uccaret SAstra padDatim /

   adhyātmagaticāreṇa kevalena viśodhikām /	aDyAtma gati cAreNa kevalena viSoDikAm /

   abhimānaṃ tathoccārya kuryādvai pūrvavattadā /	aBimAnam taTA uccArya kuryAt vE pUrvavat tadA /

   gurupāramparāyātaḥ sampradāyaḥ prakāśitaḥ /	guru pArampara AyAtaH sampradAyaH prakASitaH /

   tattvādhvānaṃ kalādhvānaṃ bhuvanādhvānameva ca // SvaT_5.86 //	tattva aDvAnam kalA aDvAnam Buvana aDvAnam eva ca // SvaT_5.86 //
   varṇamantrapadādhvānaṃ kṛtvaivaṃ śuddhyati priye /	varNa mantra pada aDvAnam kRtvA evam SudDi ati priye /

   mantrasiddhena vā devi kṛtā vai sukṛtā bhavet // SvaT_5.88 //	mantra sidDena vA devi kRtA vE sukRtA Bavet // SvaT_5.88 //
   iti svacchandatantre tattvadīkṣāprakāśanaṃ nāma pañcamaḥ paṭalaḥ	iti svacCanda tantre tattvadIkzAprakASanam nAma paQcamaH pawalaH
   ṣaṣṭhaḥ paṭalaḥ	zazWaH pawalaH
   samayācārayuktasya sādhakasya varānane /	samaya AcAra yuktasya sADakasya varAnane /
   jāyate vividhā siddhiḥ girigahvaramāśrite // SvaT_6.1 //	jAyate viviDA sidDiH giri gahvaram ASrite // SvaT_6.1 //
   suśuddhe bhūpradeśe tu sarvaśalyavivarjite /	su SudDe BU pradeSe tu sarva Salya vivarjite /
   pracchanne vijane ramye bhairavaṃ tatra pūjayet // SvaT_6.2 //	pracCanne vijane ramye BEravam tatra pUjayet // SvaT_6.2 //
   japitvākṣaralakṣaṃ tu bahurūpasya suvrate /	japitvA akzara lakzam tu bahu rUpasya suvrate /

   mucyate na tu sandeho bhedanāt praṇavasya tu /	mucyate na tu sandehaH BedanAt praNavasya tu /

   vinā praṇavasaṃyogāj jīva eko vyavasthitaḥ /	vinA praNava saMyogAt jIvaH ekaH vyavasTitaH /

   tathā ṣaṣṭhena sambhinno dehe jīvaḥ pravartate /	taTA zazWena samBinnaH dehe jIvaH pravartate /

   sa ca candrodayo devi rajanī ca vidhīyate // SvaT_7.37 //	sa ca candra udayaH devi rajanI ca viDIyate // SvaT_7.37 //

   bhaumādyāśca grahā hyevaṃ caranti pravibhāgaśaḥ /	BOma AdyAH ca grahAH hi evam caranti praviBAgaSaH /
   prāṇe cāpyudayantyete prahare prahare priye // SvaT_7.42 //	prANe ca api udayanti ete prahare prahare priye // SvaT_7.42 //

   garbhasthānekadhārūpaṃ yadgṛhītaṃ purātanam // SvaT_7.102 //	garBa sTAn ekaDA rUpam yat gRhItam purAtanam // SvaT_7.102 //
   karkaṭādeḥ samārabhya sarvaṃ varṣati tatpunaḥ /	karkawa AdeH samAraBya sarvam varzati tat punar /

   kaṇṭhādadhastato dehī hṛtpadmātsarvato vrajet /	kaNWAt aDas tatas dehI hRd padmAt sarvatas vrajet /

   tatra pūjā japo homo yatkṛtaṃ muktidaṃ bhavet /	tatra pUjA japaH homaH yat kRtam mukti dam Bavet /

   bāhye caiva tvahorātre adhyātmaṃ tu varānane /	bAhye ca eva tu ahorAtre aDyAtmam tu varAnane /
   caturviṃśatisaṃkrāntīḥ prāṇahaṃsastu saṃkramet // SvaT_7.167 //	caturviMSati saMkrAntIH prANa haMsaH tu saMkramet // SvaT_7.167 //

   pañcapañcakametaddhi kathitaṃ te varānane /	paQca paQcakam etat hi kaTitam te varAnane /

   ahaṃkāro dhīrmanaśca indriyārthāstathaiva ca /	ahaMkAraH DIH manaH ca indriya arTAH taTA eva ca /

   sūtakaṃ mṛtakaṃ tyaktvā tiṣṭhedvai tattvavṛttitaḥ /	sUtakam mRtakam tyaktvA tizWet vE tattva vRttitaH /
   tattvavṛttiśca vyākhyātā sarvādhvopādhivarjitā // SvaT_7.241 //	tattva vRttiH ca vyAKyAtA sarva aDva upADi varjitAH // SvaT_7.241 //

   samaḥ śatrau ca mitre ca brāhmaṇe śvapace samaḥ /	samaH SatrO ca mitre ca brAhmaNe Svapace samaH /

   nityaṃ tasya vaśāste vai śivabhāvanayānayā /	nityam tasya vaSAH te vE Siva BAvanayA anayA /

   kṛtakṛtyaḥ prasannātmā kṛtyaṃ cāsya na vidyate /	kRtakRtyaH prasanna AtmA kRtyam ca asya na vidyate /

   dharmādharmavinirmuktaḥ puṇyapāpavivarjitaḥ /	Darma aDarma vinirmuktaH puNya pApa vivarjitaH /
   na cāsya bhakṣyābhakṣyaṃ hi na peyāpeyameva ca // SvaT_7.248 //	na ca asya Bakzya aBakzyam hi na peyA apeyam eva ca // SvaT_7.248 //
   nāpavitraṃ hi tasyāsti na pavitraṃ hi suvrate /	na apavitram hi tasya asti na pavitram hi suvrate /
   nirapekṣo hyasau nityaṃ sarvāpekṣāvivarjitaḥ // SvaT_7.249 //	nirapekzaH hi asO nityam sarva apekzA vivarjitaH // SvaT_7.249 //
   nāsya kṣetraṃ nāsya tīrthaṃ niyamo yama eva ca /	na asya kzetram na asya tIrTam niyamaH yamaH eva ca /
   kṣetraṃ tasya parā śaktir yataḥ sarvaṃ prasūyate // SvaT_7.250 //	kzetram tasya parA SaktiH yatas sarvam prasUyate // SvaT_7.250 //

   niyamo bhāvanā nityaṃ paratattvaikatānatā /	niyamaH BAvanA nityam para tattva eka tAna tA /

   na divā jāgaraṃ kuryān na ca rātrau svapetkvacit /	na divA jAgaram kuryAt na ca rAtrO svapet kvacid /

   niṣkampaṃ kumbhakaṃ kṛtvā kāryāścābhyantarāstrayaḥ /	nizkampam kumBakam kRtvA kAryAH ca aByantarAH trayaH /

   navamastu kururnāma navavarṣādhipāḥ smṛtāḥ /	navamaH tu kuruH nAma nava varza aDipAH smRtAH /

   teṣāṃ nāmāṅkitānīha navavarṣāṇi pārvati /	tezAm nAma aFkitAni iha nava varzANi pArvati /
   nābheḥ putro mahāvīryo vṛṣabho dharmatatparaḥ // SvaT_10.280 //	nABeH putraH mahA vIryaH vRzaBaH Darma tatparaH // SvaT_10.280 //
   tasyāpi hi suto jñeyo bharatastu pratāpavān /	tasya api hi sutaH jQeyaH BarataH tu pratApavAn /
   tannamnaiva tu vijñeyaṃ bhārataṃ varṣamuttamam // SvaT_10.281 //	tat namna eva tu vijQeyam BAratam varzam uttamam // SvaT_10.281 //
   tasyāpyaṣṭau punaḥ putrā jātā kanyāparā priye /	tasya api azwO punar putrAH jAtA kanyA parA priye /
   bhārate tvaṣṭadvīpe 'tra aṣṭau putrā niveśitāḥ // SvaT_10.282 //	BArate tu azwadvIpe atra azwO putrAH niveSitAH // SvaT_10.282 //
   navamastu kumāryāhvaḥ kumāryāḥ pratipāditaḥ /	navamaH tu kumArI AhvaH kumAryAH pratipAditaH /
   teṣāṃ nāmnā tu te dvīpā bharatena prakīrtitāḥ // SvaT_10.283 //	tezAm nAmnA tu te dvIpAH Baratena prakIrtitAH // SvaT_10.283 //
   jambudvīpaṃ ca śākaṃ ca kuśaṃ krauñcaṃ ca śālmalim /	jambudvIpam ca SAkam ca kuSam krOQcam ca SAlmalim /
   gomedaṃ puṣkaraṃ caiva sapta dvīpāni pārvati // SvaT_10.284 //	gomedam puzkaram ca eva sapta dvIpAni pArvati // SvaT_10.284 //
   adhunā saṃpravakṣyāmi samudrāṃstava suvrate /	aDunA saMpravakzyAmi samudrAn= tava suvrate /
   kṣāraḥ kṣīraṃ dadhi ghṛtaṃ tathā ikṣuraso 'pi ca // SvaT_10.285 //	kzAraH kzIram daDi GRtam taTA ikzu rasaH api ca // SvaT_10.285 //
   madirodaśca svādūdaḥ samudrāḥ sapta kīrtitāḥ /	madirodaH ca svAdUdaH samudrAH sapta kIrtitAH /
   jambudvīpaṃ smṛtaṃ lakṣaṃ yojanānāṃ pramāṇataḥ // SvaT_10.286 //	jambudvIpam smRtam lakzam yojanAnAm pramANataH // SvaT_10.286 //
   parimaṇḍalato jñeyaḥ kṣārodastatsamo bahiḥ /	parimaNxalataH jQeyaH kzArodaH tad samaH bahis /

   agnīdhraśca samākhyāto jambudvīpe varānane /	agnIDraH ca samAKyAtaH jambudvIpe varAnane /

   rājā krauñce 'tha jyotiṣmān śālmalau dyutimānsmṛtaḥ /	rAjA krOQce aTa jyotizmAn SAlmalO dyutimAn smRtaH /
   gomede havyanāmā tu savanaḥ puṣkare tathā // SvaT_10.289 //	gomede havya nAmA tu savanaH puzkare taTA // SvaT_10.289 //
   tretāyugasamaḥ kālaḥ śākagomedavāsinām /	tretA yuga samaH kAlaH SAka gomeda vAsinAm /
   tathā varṇāśramācārā jñeyāstatra nivāsinām // SvaT_10.290 //	taTA varNa ASrama AcArAH jQeyAH tatra nivAsinAm // SvaT_10.290 //
   medhātitheḥ sapta putrāḥ śākadvīpe 'bhiṣecitāḥ /	meDAtiTeH sapta putrAH SAkadvIpe aBizecitAH /
   śānto 'bhayastvaśiśiraḥ sukhado nandakaḥ śivaḥ // SvaT_10.291 //	SAntaH aBayaH tu aSiSiraH suKa daH nandakaH SivaH // SvaT_10.291 //
   kṣemakaśca dhruvaśceti varṣanāmnā tu te 'ṅkitāḥ /	kzemakaH ca DruvaH ca iti varza nAmnA tu te aFkitAH /
   varṣāṇi sapta khyātāni parvatāṃśca nibodha me // SvaT_10.292 //	varzANi sapta KyAtAni parvatAn= ca niboDa me // SvaT_10.292 //
   gomedaścandrasaṃjñaśca nārado dundubhistathā /	gomedaH candra saMjQaH ca nAradaH dunduBiH taTA /

   sukṛtā cānasūyā ca sumukhī ca tṛtīyakā /	sukRtA ca anasUyA ca sumuKI ca tRtIyakAH /

   etā eva mahānadyo giriṣveteṣu nirgatāḥ /	etAH eva mahA nadyaH girizu etezu nirgatAH /

   śākadvīpe tu ye lokāḥ kṣīrāhārāḥ phalāśinaḥ /	SAkadvIpe tu ye lokAH kzIra AhArAH Pala ASinaH /

   krīḍanti divyanārībhiḥ sarvaiśvaryasamanvitāḥ /	krIxanti divya nArIBiH sarva ESvarya samanvitAH /

   kumudaścorvadaścaiva vārāho droṇakaṅkatau /	kumudaH ca urvadaH ca eva vArAhaH droNa kaFkatO /

   śvetatoyā tathā kṛṣṇā candrā śuklā ca locanī /	Sveta toyA taTA kRzNA candrA SuklA ca locanI /
   vīvṛtā ca vivṛndā ca saptaitāstu saridvarāḥ // SvaT_10.300 //	vIvRtA ca vivRndA ca sapta etAH tu sarit varAH // SvaT_10.300 //
   dadhyudakaṃ praviṣṭāstā nimnagāḥ pāvanodakāḥ /	daDi udakam pravizwAH tAH nimnagAH pAvana udakAH /
   janāstu sukhinastatra dadhnāmṛtaphalāśinaḥ // SvaT_10.301 //	janAH tu suKinaH tatra daDnA amRta Pala ASinaH // SvaT_10.301 //
   divyabhogaratāḥ sarve krīḍantyete sayoṣitaḥ /	divya Boga ratAH sarve krIxanti ete sa yozitaH /
   jyotiṣmatā sapta putrāḥ krauñcadvīpe niveśitāḥ // SvaT_10.302 //	jyotizmatA sapta putrAH krOQcadvIpe niveSitAH // SvaT_10.302 //
   udbhijjaśca samākhyāto veṇurmaṇḍala eva ca /	udBid jaH ca samAKyAtaH veNuH maNxalaH eva ca /
   rathakāraśca lavaṇo dhṛtimānsuprabhākaraḥ // SvaT_10.303 //	raTakAraH ca lavaNaH DRtimAn su praBA karaH // SvaT_10.303 //
   kapilaśceti rājāno varṣanāmnā ca te 'ṅkitāḥ /	kapilaH ca iti rAjAnaH varza nAmnA ca te aFkitAH /
   vaidrumo hemanābhaśca dyutimān puṣpadantakaḥ // SvaT_10.304 //	vEdrumaH hemanABaH ca dyutimAn puzpadantakaH // SvaT_10.304 //
   kuśalo harimardaśca saptaite tu kulādrayaḥ /	kuSalaH harimardaH ca saptA ete tu kula adrayaH /
   mahī dhātā śivāpāpā pavitrā saṃtatadyutiḥ // SvaT_10.305 //	mahI DAtA Siva apApA pavitrA saMtata dyutiH // SvaT_10.305 //
   dambhā ceti samākhyātāḥ saptaitāḥ saritaḥ srutāḥ /	damBA ca iti samAKyAtAH sapta etAH saritaH srutAH /
   ghṛtodaṃ praviśantyetāḥ sarvāḥ pāpaharāḥ priye // SvaT_10.306 //	GRta udam praviSanti etAH sarvAH pApa harAH priye // SvaT_10.306 //
   janāstadvāsinaḥ sarve surūpāstejasotkaṭāḥ /	janAH tad vAsinaH sarve surUpAH tejasA utkawAH /

   krīḍanti vanitāyuktāḥ padmapatrāyatekṣaṇāḥ /	krIxanti vanitA yuktAH padma patra Ayata IkzaNAH /
   sapta dyutimatā putrāḥ śālmalāvabhiṣecitāḥ // SvaT_10.308 //	sapta dyutimatA putrAH SAlmalO= aBizecitAH // SvaT_10.308 //
   manonugastathoṣṇaśca pāvano hyandhakārakaḥ /	manonugaH taTA uzNaH ca pAvanaH hi anDakArakaH /
   munirdundubhināmā ca kuśalaśceti te smṛtāḥ // SvaT_10.309 //	muniH dunduBi nAmA ca kuSalaH ca iti te smRtAH // SvaT_10.309 //
   varṣanāmāni teṣāṃ vai saptānāṃ sapta tu kramāt /	varza nAmAni tezAm vE saptAnAm sapta tu kramAt /
   krauñco 'tha vāmanaścaivāpy andhakāro divākṛtiḥ // SvaT_10.310 //	krOQcaH aTa vAmanaH ca eva api anDakAraH divAkRtiH // SvaT_10.310 //
   dvibinduḥ puṇḍarīkaśca dundubhiśca kulādrayaḥ /	dvibinduH puNxarIkaH ca dunduBiH ca kula adrayaH /
   pauṇḍarī kauśikī gaurī siddhā caiva kumudvatī // SvaT_10.311 //	pONxarI kOSikI gOrI sidDA ca eva kumudvatI // SvaT_10.311 //
   sandhyā rātrī ca vikhyātā samāsātparikīrtitāḥ /	sanDyA rAtrI ca viKyAtA samAsAt parikIrtitAH /
   nadyastāḥ śailaniṣkrāntā gacchantīkṣurasārṇavam // SvaT_10.312 //	nadyaH tAH SEla nizkrAntAH gacCanti ikzu rasa arNavam // SvaT_10.312 //

   sukhāhvā vāruṇī caiva somasya tu vibhāvarī /	suKAhvA vAruNI ca eva somasya tu viBAvarI /

   tathottarāyaṇaṃ tatra uttareṇa prakīrtitam /	taTA uttarAyaNam tatra uttareNa prakIrtitam /

   pitṛdevapathohyeṣa kathitastu mayā tava /	pitR deva paTaH hi eza kaTitaH tu mayA tava /

   pañcatriṃśatsmṛtāḥ koṭyo lakṣāṇekonaviṃśatiḥ /	paQcatriMSat smRtAH kowyaH lakzANekonaviMSatiH /

   saptasāgaramānaṃ tu garbhodastatsamaḥ smṛtaḥ /	sapta sAgara mAnam tu garBodaH tad samaH smRtaH /
   brahmaṇo 'ṇḍakaṭāhena yuktā vai merumadhyataḥ // SvaT_10.342 //	brahmaNaH aNxa kawAhena yuktAH vE meru maDyatas // SvaT_10.342 //
   pañcāśatkoṭayo jñeyā daśadikṣu samantataḥ /	paQcASat kowayaH jQeyAH daSa dikzu samantataH /
   evametacchataṃ jñeyaṃ koṭīnāṃ pārthivaṃ mahat // SvaT_10.343 //	evam etat Satam jQeyam kowInAm pArTivam mahat // SvaT_10.343 //
   ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi pramāṇaṃ varavarṇini /	atas UrDvam pravakzyAmi pramANam varavarNini /
   atha vātra mahādevi paripāṭyā samantataḥ // SvaT_10.344 //	aTa vA atra mahAdevi paripAwyA samantataH // SvaT_10.344 //
   dīkṣākāle tu saṃskārāḥ kramaṃ teṣāṃ nibodha me /	dIkzA kAle tu saMskArAH kramam tezAm niboDa me /
   śaktiṃ tattvaṃ ca bhuvanaṃ yoniṃ caiva niveśayet // SvaT_10.345 //	Saktim tattvam ca Buvanam yonim ca eva niveSayet // SvaT_10.345 //

   bhairava uvāca	BEravaH uvAca

   jagatsaṃbhavahetuśca tvatprasādācchrutaṃ mayā // SvaT_12.1 //	jagat saMBava hetuH ca tvad prasAdAt Srutam mayA // SvaT_12.1 //

   baddhaḥ saṃsarate bhūyo yāvaddevaṃ na vindati // SvaT_12.51 //	badDaH saMsarate BUyas yAvat devam na vindati // SvaT_12.51 //

   yuddhaṃ dyutaṃ tathā māyāṃ cauryaṃ cānṛtahiṃsanam /	yudDam dyutam taTA mAyAm cOryam ca anRta hiMsanam /

   ahaṃ kartā ca bhoktā ca īśvarobalavānaham /	aham kartA ca BoktA ca ISvaraH balavAn aham /

   dhyānātsiddhimavāpnoti niyateśca vimucyate /	DyAnAt sidDim avApnoti niyateH ca vimucyate /
   trinetraṃ ca caturvaktraṃ kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ caturbhujam // SvaT_12.114 //	trinetram ca catur vaktram kRzNa varNam catur Bujam // SvaT_12.114 //

   chummakāḥ sampravakṣyāmi sādhakasya varānane // SvaT_15.1 //	CummakAH sampravakzyAmi sADakasya varAnane // SvaT_15.1 //
   bhairavastu smṛto dhāma sarvadastu guruḥ smṛtaḥ /	BEravaH tu smRtaH DAma sarva daH tu guruH smRtaH /
   sādhakastu girirjñeyaḥ putrako vimalaḥ smṛtaḥ // SvaT_15.2 //	sADakaH tu giriH jQeyaH putrakaH vimalaH smRtaH // SvaT_15.2 //
   samayī kāntadehastu bhaginyo baladarpitāḥ /	samayI kAnta dehaH tu BaginyaH bala darpitAH /
   madyaṃ tu harṣaṇaṃ jñeyaṃ muditā tu surā smṛtā // SvaT_15.3 //	madyam tu harzaNam jQeyam muditA tu surA smRtAH // SvaT_15.3 //
   matysā jalacarā jñeyā māṃsaṃ ca balavardhanam /	matysA jalacarAH jQeyA mAMsam ca bala varDanam /
   jātaṃ prarūḍhamityāhur mṛtaṃ caiva parāṅmukham // SvaT_15.4 //	jAtam prarUXam iti AhuH mRtam ca eva parAFmuKam // SvaT_15.4 //
   raktaṃ tvamṛtamityāhuḥ padmanālo 'ntrasañcayaḥ /	raktam tu amRtam iti AhuH padma nAlaH antra saQcayaH /
   śukraṃ candraḥ samākhyātaḥ snāyuḥ sūtraṃ prakīrtitam // SvaT_15.5 //	Sukram candraH samAKyAtaH snAyuH sUtram prakIrtitam // SvaT_15.5 //
   śmaśānaṃ ḍāmaraṃ jñeyaṃ rākṣasastu bhayaṅkaraḥ /	SmaSAnam xAmaram jQeyam rAkzasaH tu BayaFkaraH /
   piśāco romajananaḥ ruhā jñeyā rajasvalā // SvaT_15.6 //	piSAcaH roma jananaH ruhA jQeyA rajasvalAH // SvaT_15.6 //
   rātriṃ vai cchādikāṃ viddhi prakāśaśca dinaṃ bhavet /	rAtrim vE cCA AdikAm vidDi prakASaH ca dinam Bavet /
   nayane cañcale jñeye jihvāṃ saṃgrāhikāṃ viduḥ // SvaT_15.7 //	nayane caQcale jQeye jihvAm saMgrAhikAm viduH // SvaT_15.7 //
   karau dhanakarau jñeyau pādau sahacarau viduḥ /	karO Dana karO jQeyO pAdO sahacarO viduH /
   liṅgaṃ santoṣajananaṃ bhagaḥ prītivivardhanaḥ // SvaT_15.8 //	liFgam santoza jananam BagaH prIti vivarDanaH // SvaT_15.8 //
   śastraṃ vibhāgajananaṃ kartarī kāryasādhikā /	Sastram viBAga jananam kartarI kArya sADikAH /
   dūtī saṃvāhikā jñeyā dhūpo hlādana ucyate // SvaT_15.9 //	dUtI saMvAhikAH jQeyAH DUpaH hlAdanaH ucyate // SvaT_15.9 //
   gandhaḥ santoṣajanano rājāno dhārakāḥ smṛtāḥ /	ganDaH santoza jananaH rAjAnaH DArakAH smRtAH /
   paśurvibodhako jñeyaś carukaḥ sārvakāmikaḥ // SvaT_15.10 //	paSuH viboDakaH jQeyaH carukaH sArvakAmikaH // SvaT_15.10 //
   annaṃ sādhanamityuktaṃ vasā maṇḍamihocyate /	annam sADanam iti uktam vasA maNxam iha ucyate /
   diśāṃ mukhaṃ tu śravaṇaṃ tvak ca saṃvedanī smṛtā // SvaT_15.11 //	diSAm muKam tu SravaNam tvac ca saMvedanI smRtAH // SvaT_15.11 //
   ghrāṇaṃ susthitamityuktaṃ mukhaṃ tu pravicārakam /	GrANam susTitam iti uktam muKam tu pravicArakam /
   paśu pracāro vijñeyaḥ mātā dhātrīti kathyate // SvaT_15.12 //	paSu pracAraH vijQeyaH mAtA DAtrI iti kaTyate // SvaT_15.12 //
   pitaraṃ sṛṣṭikartāraṃ bhrātaraṃ pālakaṃ viduḥ /	pitaram sRzwi kartAram BrAtaram pAlakam viduH /
   bhaginī śubhakarī jñeyā sakhī sarvārthasādhikā // SvaT_15.13 //	BaginI SuBa karI jQeyA saKI sarva arTa sADikAH // SvaT_15.13 //
   mitraṃ guṇānāṃ jananaṃ guṇanāśaṃ ripuṃ viduḥ /	mitram guNAnAm jananam guNa nASam ripum viduH /
   chit sphijau kīrtito devi dṛṣṭiścakṣuḥ prakīrtitam // SvaT_15.14 //	CiD sPijO kIrtitaH devi dRzwiH cakzuH prakIrtitam // SvaT_15.14 //
   daśanāḥ khaṇḍakā jñeyā ādhāra udaraṃ smṛtam /	daSanAH KaNxakAH jQeyAH ADAraH udaram smRtam /
   hṛdayaṃ guhyamityuktaṃ kaṭhinaṃ tvasthi viddhi hi // SvaT_15.15 //	hRdayam guhyam iti uktam kaWinam tu asTi vidDi hi // SvaT_15.15 //
   medo vasāṃ vijānīyāt majjā puṣṭikaraḥ smṛtaḥ /	medaH vasAm vijAnIyAt majjA puzwi karaH smRtaH /
   viṣṭhāṃ vidūṣikāṃ viddhi mūtraṃ snāva ihocyate // SvaT_15.16 //	vizWAm vidUzikAm vidDi mUtram snAvaH iha ucyate // SvaT_15.16 //
   kāleyakaṃ tu kusumaṃ dhūmaṃ dhṛtikaraṃ viduḥ /	kAleyakam tu kusumam DUmam DRti karam viduH /
   melakaṃ caiva saṅghātaḥ putraḥ soddyotakaḥ smṛtaḥ // SvaT_15.17 //	melakam ca eva saFGAtaH putraH sa uddyotakaH smRtaH // SvaT_15.17 //
   duhitā hlādikā jñeyā kṣubdhaṃ vai calitaṃ viduḥ /	duhitA hlAdikAH jQeyA kzubDam vE calitam viduH /
   dūṣako jāra ityuktaḥ pītaṃ vanditameva ca // SvaT_15.18 //	dUzakaH jAraH iti uktaH pItam vanditam eva ca // SvaT_15.18 //
   bhakṣitaṃ prāptamityāhuś charditaṃ vikṛtīkṛtam /	Bakzitam prAptam iti AhuH Carditam vikRtIkRtam /
   dūṣitaṃ karṣitaṃ jñeyaṃ sammataṃ samayaṃ viduḥ // SvaT_15.19 //	dUzitam karzitam jQeyam sammatam samayam viduH // SvaT_15.19 //
   mahallo rakṣako jñeyaś chagalastu kaniṣṭhakaḥ /	mahallaH rakzakaH jQeyaH CagalaH tu kanizWakaH /
   vinayo dehakarma syāt sādhanaṃ tu japaḥ smṛtaḥ // SvaT_15.20 //	vinayaH deha karma syAt sADanam tu japaH smRtaH // SvaT_15.20 //
   homitaṃ siddhijananaṃ vibhāgo rocakaḥ smṛtaḥ /	homitam sidDi jananam viBAgaH rocakaH smRtaH /
   kadambaṃ vṛndamityāhur viralo 'śliṣṭa ucyate // SvaT_15.21 //	kadambam vRndam iti AhuH viralaH aSlizwaH ucyate // SvaT_15.21 //
   vimalaḥ śiṣya ityukta icchā cājñā prakīrtitā /	vimalaH SizyaH iti uktaH icCA ca AjQA prakIrtitA /
   devatādarśanaṃ yattat labdhaṃ śastrahataṃ viduḥ // SvaT_15.22 //	devatA darSanam yat tat labDam Sastra hatam viduH // SvaT_15.22 //
   niśācaro biḍālaḥ syāt nakhinaśca vidārakāḥ /	niSAcaraH bixAlaH syAt naKinaH ca vidArakAH /
   ānītaṃ sāritaṃ jñeyaṃ rakṣitaṃ pihitaṃ tathā // SvaT_15.23 //	AnItam sAritam jQeyam rakzitam pihitam taTA // SvaT_15.23 //
   śikhāṃ saṃspṛśate yā tu sā tu śaktiṃ vinirdiśet /	SiKAm saMspRSate yA tu sA tu Saktim vinirdiSet /
   śiraḥ pradarśayedyā tu sā ca binduṃ vinirdiśet // SvaT_15.24 //	SiraH pradarSayet yA tu sA ca bindum vinirdiSet // SvaT_15.24 //
   lalāṭaṃ darśayedyā tu īśvaraṃ sā vinirdiśet /	lalAwam darSayet yA tu ISvaram sA vinirdiSet /
   tālukaṃ darśayedyā tu tayā rudraḥ prakīrtitaḥ // SvaT_15.25 //	tAlukam darSayet yA tu tayA rudraH prakIrtitaH // SvaT_15.25 //
   jihvāṃ pradarśayedyā tu vidyāṃ sātha vinirdiśet /	jihvAm pradarSayet yA tu vidyAm sA aTa vinirdiSet /
   sapta koṭayastu mantrāṇāṃ tasyā jñeyāstu suvrate // SvaT_15.26 //	sapta kowayaH tu mantrANAm tasyAH jQeyAH tu suvrate // SvaT_15.26 //
   ghaṇṭikāṃ darśayedyā tu tasyānantaḥ pradarśitaḥ /	GaNwikAm darSayet yA tu tasya anantaH pradarSitaH /
   kaṇṭhaṃ tu saṃspṛśeyā sā kālatattvaṃ vinirdiśet // SvaT_15.27 //	kaNWam tu saMspRSeyA sA kAla tattvam vinirdiSet // SvaT_15.27 //
   hṛtpadmaṃ darśayedyā tu puruṣaṃ sā vinirdiśet /	hRd padmam darSayet yA tu puruzam sA vinirdiSet /
   nābhiṃ pradarśayedyā tu prakṛtiṃ sā vinirdiśet // SvaT_15.28 //	nABim pradarSayet yA tu prakRtim sA vinirdiSet // SvaT_15.28 //
   tasyādhastād buddhitattvaṃ yadi syāddarśanaṃ priye /	tasya aDastAt budDi tattvam yadi syAt darSanam priye /
   yadā guhyaṃ spṛśeddevi ahaṃkāro 'dhidaivatam // SvaT_15.29 //	yadA guhyam spRSet devi ahaMkAraH aDidEvatam // SvaT_15.29 //
   kaṭiṃ sandarśayedyā tu vyoma tatrādhidhaivatam /	kawim sandarSayet yA tu vyoma tatra aDiDEvatam /
   ūrukau darśayeddevi pavanaṃ sā vinirdiśet // SvaT_15.30 //	UrukO darSayet devi pavanam sA vinirdiSet // SvaT_15.30 //
   jānunī darśayedyā tu tayā tejaḥ prakīrtitam /	jAnunI darSayet yA tu tayA tejaH prakIrtitam /
   jaṅghe pradarśayedyā tu varuṇaṃ sā vinirdiśet // SvaT_15.31 //	jaFGe pradarSayet yA tu varuNam sA vinirdiSet // SvaT_15.31 //
   śarīraṃ darśayeddevi sarvavedamayaṃ priye /	SarIram darSayet devi sarva veda mayam priye /
   pūjāgnijapayuktasya dhyānayuktasya mantriṇaḥ // SvaT_15.32 //	pUjA agni japa yuktasya DyAna yuktasya mantriNaH // SvaT_15.32 //
   samayācārayuktasya kālāṃśakavidaḥ priye /	samaya AcAra yuktasya kAla aMSa ka vidaH priye /
   kriyopetasya deveśi yoginyastu varapradāḥ // SvaT_15.33 //	kriyA upetasya deveSi yoginyaH tu vara pradAH // SvaT_15.33 //
   darśayanti mahādhvānaṃ nānābhogasamanvitam /	darSayanti mahA DvAnam nAnA Boga samanvitam /
   girirājasya deveśi yaṃ gatvā phalamaśnute // SvaT_15.34 //	girirAjasya deveSi yam gatvA Palam aSnute // SvaT_15.34 //
   bhairaveṇa samājñaptāḥ śaktayastu varānane /	BEraveNa samAjQaptAH SaktayaH tu varAnane /
   anyāśca siddhīrvividhā adhamā madhyamottamāḥ // SvaT_15.35 //	anyAH ca sidDIH viviDAH aDamAH maDyama uttamAH // SvaT_15.35 //
   anyatantrasamutthāśca sādhayanti na saṃśayaḥ /	anya tantra samutTAH ca sADayanti na saMSayaH /
   evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ melakaṃ tu varānane // SvaT_15.36 //	evam saMkzepataH proktam melakam tu varAnane // SvaT_15.36 //
   satatābhyāsayogena dadate carukaṃ svakam /	satata aByAsa yogena dadate carukam svakam /
   yasya samprāśanāddevi vīreśasadṛśo bhavet // SvaT_15.37 //	yasya samprASanAt devi vIreSa sadRSaH Bavet // SvaT_15.37 //
   tasmād dhyānārcane homaṃ japam ca varavarṇini /	tasmAt DyAna arcane homam japam ca varavarNini /
   kurvanti bhāvitātmānas tataḥ siddhyanti mantriṇaḥ // SvaT_15.38 //	kurvanti BAvitAtmAnaH tatas sidDyanti mantriNaH // SvaT_15.38 //
   iti svacchandatantre pañcadaśaḥ paṭalaḥ	iti svacCanda tantre paQcadaSaH pawalaH
